Task ID: 1
Agent: main (Z.ai Code orchestrator)
Task: Build Phase 1 of a premium calculator web app (Next.js, TypeScript, Tailwind) with a dark-navy + gold glassmorphism theme, full keyboard support, live expression preview, and copy-to-clipboard.

Work Log:
- Explored the existing Next.js 16 + Tailwind CSS 4 + shadcn/ui scaffold (package.json, globals.css, layout.tsx, toaster).
- Created `src/lib/calculator.ts` — pure logic: tokenizer (handles ASCII + display operators, unary minus, scientific notation), shunting-yard → RPN evaluator with operator precedence, divide-by-zero guard, `formatResult`, `formatExpressionForDisplay`, `computePreview`, `lastNumberSegment`.
- Created `src/hooks/useCalculator.ts` — all state + actions (digit, decimal, operator, percent, backspace, clear, allClear, evaluate, copyResult), live preview via useMemo, full keyboard handler (0-9, + - * /, ., %, Enter/=, Backspace, Escape, c), clipboard with themed toast.
- Created `src/components/calculator/CalculatorButton.tsx` — button with gold-glow ripple animation on pointer down, 4 variants (number/operator/function/equals), tabIndex=-1 to avoid Enter/equals focus conflict.
- Created `src/components/calculator/Display.tsx` — expression preview (top, muted), large gold-gradient result (Space Grotesk, auto-shrinking size), copy button with check confirmation, inline error chip.
- Created `src/components/calculator/Keypad.tsx` — 4×5 grid (AC, C, ⌫, ÷ / 7 8 9 × / 4 5 6 − / 1 2 3 + / % 0 . =).
- Created `src/components/calculator/Calculator.tsx` — glassmorphism card assembling Display + Keypad with a gold divider.
- Rewrote `src/app/page.tsx` — navy page shell with ambient gold glows, AURIC header badge, Calculator, sticky footer with keyboard-hint chips.
- Rewrote `src/app/layout.tsx` — added Space Grotesk display font, premium metadata.
- Rewrote `src/app/globals.css` — appended unlayered premium theme: navy body bg, glass card (gradient + gold border-glow + backdrop blur + ::before gradient ring), button variants, ripple keyframes, gold-gradient result text, kbd chips, themed toast.
- Wrote `README.md` with features, tech stack, keyboard shortcuts, project structure, deployment notes.

Verification & Fixes:
- Ran `bun run lint` — clean, no errors/warnings.
- Restarted dev server (Turbopack CSS HMR was serving stale globals.css; a fresh `rm -rf .next` + `(bun run dev &)` detach fixed it).
- Used Agent Browser for end-to-end verification:
  - Rendered correctly (title, 20 buttons with ARIA labels, navy bg #0a0e17, glass card gradient + gold border + gold shadow, Space Grotesk font, gold-gradient result text).
  - Computed styles confirmed all premium theme tokens applied.
  - 25 + 30 × 2 = 85 (precedence correct).
  - Caught & fixed a critical bug: `normalizeOperator` mapped ASCII `*` and `/` to `+` (missing switch cases) — added `case "*"` and `case "/"`.
  - = commits result, expression shows trailing "=".
  - Copy-to-clipboard shows check icon + themed toast (verified `<li data-state="open">` in the toast viewport).
  - Keyboard: 5 / 0 Enter → "Cannot divide by zero" inline error; Escape clears it.
  - Decimals: 12.5 + 7.5 = 20.
  - Percent: 50% = 0.5.
  - Backspace: 123 → 12.
  - Continue after =: 5+3=8, ×2 → 8 × 2 → 16.
  - Clear entry (c): 999 + 4 → 999 +.
  - Responsive: mobile 375×812 (card 343px, no horizontal scroll, footer at bottom) and desktop 1280×900 (400px centered card, footer sticky/pushed on overflow).
- VLM (z-ai vision) analyzed a screenshot: confirmed "distinctly premium and fintech-like, not generic or templated" — deep navy background, glass card with thin gold border + ambient shadows, gold equals button with glow, gold result display.

Stage Summary:
- Phase 1 complete and browser-verified. All core functionality working: +, −, ×, ÷ with precedence, C/AC, decimal, backspace, %, full keyboard, live expression preview, divide-by-zero + invalid expression handling (inline), copy-to-clipboard with toast.
- Premium dark-navy + gold glassmorphism design verified via computed styles and VLM analysis.
- Clean component structure (Display, Keypad, CalculatorButton, Calculator), `useCalculator` hook owns all logic, pure `calculator.ts` lib, full TypeScript types (no `any`), lint clean.
- Dev server running on port 3000, no runtime errors/hydration warnings in dev.log.
- Single user-visible route `/` only. Ready for Vercel deployment.

Task ID: 2
Agent: main (Z.ai Code orchestrator)
Task: Build Phase 2 of the premium navy/gold calculator — mode tabs, scientific mode, memory functions, history panel (localStorage), undo/redo — extending Phase 1 without changing the visual identity.

Work Log:
- Read Phase 1 worklog + existing files (calculator.ts, useCalculator.ts, components) to plan a non-breaking extension.
- Extended `src/lib/calculator.ts`: added constants (π, e), functions (sin/cos/tan/sqrt/log/ln), parentheses, power `^` (right-associative), factorial `!` (postfix), deg/rad `AngleMode`, `genId()`. Rewrote tokenizer (word-reading for function names, strict scientific-notation parsing so standalone `e` stays a constant) and shunting-yard evaluator (functions, parens, postfix !/%, right-assoc ^). Extended `formatExpressionForDisplay` for `^`, `!`, function names. `evaluateExpression`/`computePreview` now take `angleMode`.
- Created `src/hooks/useHistory.ts` — history store backed by `useSyncExternalStore` (SSR-safe, lint-compliant). Items persisted to `localStorage` (`auric:history:v1`), capped at 100. `add`/`remove`/`clear`/`updateLabel` (80-char label limit). Cross-tab sync via `storage` event.
- Rewrote `src/hooks/useCalculator.ts` with `useReducer` (present + undo/redo stacks, COMPUTE/UNDO/REDO actions) so all action callbacks are stable (depend only on `dispatch`). Added: mode, angleMode, memory/hasMemory, lastEvaluation, and actions inputFunction/inputConstant/inputParen/inputPower/inputFactorial/memoryAdd/Subtract/Recall/Clear/undo/redo/loadResult/toggleAngleMode. Implicit `*` inserted when appending a value after a value-ending token (e.g. `5π`→`5*π`, `2(`→`2*(`). Backspace removes a whole `name(` function token. Refs (present/angleMode/memory/hasMemory) written only inside effects. Extended keyboard handler with `(` `)` `^` `!` and Ctrl/Cmd+Z / Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+Z / Ctrl+Y.
- Created `src/components/calculator/ModeTabs.tsx` — Standard/Scientific tabs with a CSS-transform sliding gold indicator (`data-mode`).
- Created `src/components/calculator/MemoryBar.tsx` — M+/M−/MR/MC + gold memory indicator (active dot when value stored). Visible in both modes.
- Created `src/components/calculator/ScientificKeypad.tsx` — 4-col grid: DEG/RAD (span2), sin, cos, tan, √, xʸ, log, ln, x!, (, ), π (span2), e (span2).
- Created `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx` — slide-out glass panel: header + count, clear-all (two-tap confirm), list of items (inline editable note input, expression, = result, hover delete button), empty state. Clicking an item body reuses its result; backdrop click closes.
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/Calculator.tsx` — orchestrates topbar (ModeTabs + undo/redo/history utils), Display, MemoryBar, divider, optional ScientificKeypad + divider, Keypad, and HistoryPanel. Wires `calc.lastEvaluation` → `history.add` via an effect keyed on the evaluation id (deps: id + stable `addHistory`).
- Updated `src/components/calculator/Display.tsx` — added a subtle DEG/RAD chip (scientific mode only) on the expression line; Phase 1 layout unchanged in standard mode.
- Appended Phase 2 styles to `src/app/globals.css` — tabs + sliding indicator, util buttons, memory bar + indicator, scientific card width, history panel (backdrop, slide transform, header, items, note input, scrollbar, empty state). All in the established navy/gold glassmorphism language.
- Updated `src/app/page.tsx` footer text to "Phase 2 · Standard & Scientific · Memory · History · Undo/Redo".
- Updated `README.md` with Phase 2 features, extended keyboard table, and the new file structure.

Verification & Fixes:
- ESLint initially flagged: (a) ref-writes-during-render, (b) setState-in-effect, (c) unused eslint-disable. Resolved by refactoring useCalculator to useReducer (no render-time ref writes), replacing useHistory's effect-hydration with `useSyncExternalStore`, and removing the unused disable.
- Caught a critical runtime bug via Agent Browser: clicking `=` caused a "Maximum update depth exceeded" crash. Root cause: the Calculator effect depended on the `history` object (a new reference every render) → effect fired every render → `history.add` → re-render → infinite loop. Fixed by destructuring the stable `add` callback (`addHistory`) and depending on `[calc.lastEvaluation?.id, addHistory]`.
- The crash had polluted localStorage with 100 duplicate items (from the loop); cleared via `localStorage.removeItem` and re-verified clean behavior (exactly N items after N evaluations).
- Agent Browser end-to-end verification (all passed):
  - Phase 1 regression: 25+30×2=85, 5/0→"Cannot divide by zero", 12.5+7.5=20, 50%=0.5, backspace, continue-after-equals, AC — all intact.
  - Mode tabs: sliding indicator switches Standard↔Scientific; scientific buttons (sin/π/DEG…) appear/disappear; standard mode shows exactly 20 buttons.
  - Scientific: sin(90) DEG=1, sin(90) RAD=0.894 (DEG/RAD toggle works), √16=4, 2^3=8, 2^3^2=512 (right-assoc), 5!=120, 2π=6.283… (implicit mult), (2+3)×4=20 (parens+precedence), e=2.718…
  - Memory: M+ (8), M− (8−2=6), MR recalls 6, MC clears (MC/MR disabled when empty), gold indicator active when stored.
  - Undo/Redo: 123→undo→12→undo→1→redo→12; 2^3=8→undo→"2^3"(preview 8)→redo→"2^3 ="(evaluated); Ctrl+Z / Ctrl+Shift+Z keyboard shortcuts work.
  - History: panel opens/closes (slide), records exactly one item per `=`, click item reuses result + closes panel, inline note ("Rent calculation"/"Test note") saved, delete item, clear-all (two-tap confirm + empty state), persists across page reload (items + notes).
  - Keyboard: `(` `)` `^` `!` + all Phase 1 keys; Ctrl/Cmd+Z undo, Ctrl/Cmd+Shift+Z & Ctrl/Cmd+Y redo.
  - Responsive: mobile 375×812 (card 343px, no h-scroll, footer at bottom); desktop 1280×900 (400px centered card, scientific 2 grids, history panel open, footer at bottom).
  - VLM (z-ai vision) analyzed a scientific-mode + history screenshot: "cohesive, premium, and thematically consistent" — scientific buttons, history panel, and gold sliding tab all match the established navy/gold glassmorphism identity (not tacked-on).
- Final `bun run lint` clean; dev.log shows no errors/warnings; browser console clean (only HMR/React DevTools info).

Stage Summary:
- Phase 2 complete and browser-verified. All requested features working: Standard/Scientific mode tabs (sliding gold indicator), scientific functions (sin/cos/tan + DEG/RAD, √, xʸ, log, ln, x!, parentheses, π, e), memory (M+/M−/MR/MC + indicator, both modes), history panel (slide-out glass, reuse, notes, delete, clear-all, localStorage persistence), undo/redo (buttons + Ctrl+Z/Ctrl+Shift+Z).
- Phase 1 functionality fully preserved (verified by regression suite). Visual identity unchanged — same dark navy + gold glassmorphism, fonts, and button style.
- Clean architecture: `useCalculator` (useReducer, all logic + undo/redo), separate `useHistory` (useSyncExternalStore + localStorage), presentational components (ModeTabs, MemoryBar, ScientificKeypad, HistoryPanel, Display, Keypad, CalculatorButton, Calculator). Full TypeScript, no `any`, lint clean.
- Dev server running on port 3000, no runtime/console errors. Single user-visible route `/`. Vercel-ready.

Task ID: 1
Agent: general-purpose (pure-logic libs + tests)
Task: Create converters.ts, nlp.ts, algebra.ts and unit tests for the calculator engine.

Work Log:
- Read `worklog.md` (Phase 1 & 2 history) and `src/lib/calculator.ts` to learn the existing engine API: `evaluateExpression(expr, angleMode)`, `formatResult(value)`, `CalculatorError`, `AngleMode`, plus tokenizer/RPN internals (handles + - * / ^ ! %, parens, sin/cos/tan/sqrt/log/ln, π, e, deg/rad). Confirmed `@/*` path alias is wired in tsconfig.
- Created `src/lib/converters.ts`: `ConverterCategory` type, `Unit`/`CategoryDef` interfaces, `CATEGORIES` constant (length: mm/cm/m/km/in/ft/yd/mi; weight: mg/g/kg/t/oz/lb; temperature: °C/°F/K). `convertUnit(category, fromId, toId, value)` — length/weight via base-unit factors (meters/grams), temperature via explicit C↔F↔K formulas. Throws `CalculatorError` on invalid ids / non-finite values. `formatConverted(value)` reuses `formatResult` with a finiteness guard.
- Created `src/lib/nlp.ts`: `ParsedInput` interface, `parseNaturalInput(text, angleMode)` that lowercases, trims, drops leading "what is"/"calculate"/"equals"/"=", removes thousands separators, then applies phrase regexes in order — percent-off (`X% off Y` → `(Y*(1-X/100))`), percent-of (`X[%] of Y` → `(X/100*Y)` with `\bof\b` to avoid matching "off"), sqrt-of (`sqrt of X`/`square root of X` → `sqrt(X)`, parens optional) — then word operators (plus/minus/times/multiplied by/product of/divided by/over/to the power of/power of; mod intentionally skipped), then π/e normalization (standalone `e` via `\be\b` preserves scientific notation), then strips spaces and calls `evaluateExpression`+`formatResult`. Wraps any eval failure in `CalculatorError("Could not understand that expression")`. Also exports `looksLikeEquation(text)` — true when text has `=` AND a letter a-z that isn't part of a reserved function/constant word.
- Created `src/lib/algebra.ts`: `Solution` interface, `solveEquation(equation)`. Splits on `=` (requires exactly 2 sides). Detects the single variable letter (ignoring reserved function/constant words; throws if 0 or >1 distinct). Custom tokenizer (numbers, the variable letter, `^`, `*`, `+`, `-`) + recursive-descent parser builds `{ coeff, power }` terms per side, with implicit multiplication (`2x`, `3x^2`, `xx`→x²). Combines LHS − RHS into per-power coefficients; throws if any power > 2. Quadratic branch (a ≠ 0): discriminant < 0 → "No real solution"; else returns both roots joined by ", " (single root if discriminant ≈ 0). Linear branch: a=0 & b=0 → "Infinite solutions" / "No solution"; otherwise x = −c/b. Uses `formatResult` for the numeric display.
- Created `src/lib/__tests__/calculator.test.ts` (14 tests), `converters.test.ts` (11 tests), `nlp.test.ts` (6 tests), `algebra.test.ts` (5 tests) using `bun:test`. Tests use `toBe` for exact values, `toBeCloseTo` for floats (mile→m, lb→kg, 0°C→K), and `toThrow(CalculatorError)` for divide-by-zero and the no-solution equation.
- Ran `bun test src/lib/__tests__/` — all 36 tests pass across 4 files (39 expect() calls, 161ms). Ran `bun run lint` — clean, no errors or warnings.

Stage Summary:
- Files created (7, all new — no existing files modified): `src/lib/converters.ts`, `src/lib/nlp.ts`, `src/lib/algebra.ts`, `src/lib/__tests__/calculator.test.ts`, `src/lib/__tests__/converters.test.ts`, `src/lib/__tests__/nlp.test.ts`, `src/lib/__tests__/algebra.test.ts`.
- Test results: `36 pass, 0 fail, 39 expect() calls, Ran 36 tests across 4 files. [161.00ms]`.
- Lint: clean (`eslint .` exits 0, no output).
- All libs reuse the existing engine (`evaluateExpression`, `formatResult`, `CalculatorError`, `AngleMode`) via `@/lib/calculator` — no evaluation logic was reimplemented. Full TypeScript types, no `any`, no React/DOM dependencies. The three libs are pure-logic and ready to be wired into Phase 3 UI (converter panel, NL input bar, algebra solver).

Task ID: 3
Agent: Claude (chat)
Task: Continue the currency/converter work (wider currency coverage incl. PKR, searchable region-grouped picker) and fix the history export feature so users can download in every common format.

Work Log:
- Read the full project (worklog.md, src/) to understand current state: Standard/Scientific calculator, themes/settings, memory, history, undo/redo were all already complete and browser-verified in earlier tasks. The currency converter, however, was still on `frankfurter.app` (ECB-based, ~30 currencies, no PKR/INR-region coverage) with a flat hardcoded `<select>`.
- Created `src/lib/currencyData.ts` — static metadata (name, region, flag emoji) for ~90 world currencies grouped into 10 regions (South Asia, East Asia, Southeast Asia, Middle East, Central Asia, Europe, Africa, North America, South America, Oceania), plus a pinned/popular list (USD, PKR, EUR, GBP, INR, SAR, AED, CNY).
- Rewrote `src/app/api/currency/route.ts` — switched primary rate source to `open.er-api.com` (free, no key, ~160 currencies incl. PKR/BDT/LKR/NPR), with automatic fallback to the old `frankfurter.app` source if the primary is ever unreachable. Same 1-hour in-memory cache shape as before, so no other code needed to change.
- Created `src/components/calculator/CurrencySelect.tsx` — a searchable, region-grouped currency combobox (flag + code trigger button, search input, "Popular" section + per-region sections, click-outside/Escape to close). Matches the existing navy/gold glass design language exactly (reused `--c-surface-rgb`/`--c-accent-rgb`/etc. tokens).
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/Converter.tsx` — both currency selects now use `CurrencySelect` instead of native `<select>`s; default target currency is now PKR (falls back to first available code if PKR is somehow missing); removed the old hardcoded `CURRENCY_LABELS` map (now sourced from `currencyData.ts`).
- Appended `.calc-csel-*` CSS rules to `globals.css` for the new picker (trigger, dropdown panel, search bar, grouped list, empty state) — same glass/gold visual language as the rest of the app.
- Extended `src/lib/exportHistory.ts` — added `exportHistoryTxt` (plain-text, human-readable), `exportHistoryJson` (full-fidelity JSON backup), and `exportHistoryXlsx` (real .xlsx via SheetJS, dynamically imported so the library isn't in the initial bundle). Existing `exportHistoryCsv`/`exportHistoryPdf` untouched, refactored to share a `historyRows()` helper.
- Added the `xlsx` (SheetJS) package to `package.json` via `npm install xlsx --save`.
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx` — replaced the two flat CSV/PDF buttons with a single "Download" dropdown menu (click outside / re-click to close) listing all 5 formats: CSV, Excel (.xlsx), JSON, Text (.txt), PDF. Added matching `.calc-export-menu`/`.calc-export-dropdown`/`.calc-export-item` CSS.
- While in `Converter.tsx`, also fixed a pre-existing lint issue in `UnitConverter` (`setFrom`/`setTo` were being set inside a `useEffect` keyed on `catDef`, which ESLint's `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect` flags) by moving that logic into the category-tab click handler (`selectCategory`) instead — no behavior change, just removes an unnecessary effect.
- Also avoided the same lint pattern in the new `CurrencySelect.tsx` by resetting the search query directly in the open/close handlers rather than in an effect.

Verification & Fixes:
- `npx tsc --noEmit` — zero errors in any file this task touched (pre-existing unrelated errors only in `examples/websocket/*` and `bun:test` type files, both untouched by this task and irrelevant to the Next.js/Vercel build).
- `npx eslint` on every changed file — clean, zero errors/warnings.
- Attempted `npm run build` in this environment — it fails only because this sandbox's network egress does not allow `fonts.googleapis.com` (Next.js's `next/font/google` needs to fetch Geist/Geist Mono/Space Grotesk at build time). This is a sandbox network restriction, not a code defect — `layout.tsx`'s Google Fonts import predates this task, and Vercel's build environment has normal internet access, so this will build fine there. Recommend running `npm run build` once on Vercel (or any environment with open internet) to get a full build-time confirmation; type-check and lint are both clean in the meantime.
- Could not browser-verify visually in this session (no dev-server/browser tooling available here); recommend a quick manual check after deploy: open the Currency tab, confirm PKR appears and is searchable/selectable, and confirm the History panel's "Download" menu produces valid files in all 5 formats.

Stage Summary:
- Currency converter now has wide real-world coverage (~160 currencies incl. PKR, BDT, LKR, NPR, and all major regions) via a free key-less API with an automatic fallback, presented through a searchable, flag + region-grouped picker consistent with the app's premium navy/gold identity.
- History export now supports 5 formats — CSV, Excel (.xlsx), JSON, TXT, and PDF — via a single compact "Download" dropdown, resolving the earlier gap where only CSV/PDF were available.
- All new/changed files pass `tsc --noEmit` and `eslint` with zero errors. Full `npm run build` verification is pending an environment with internet access to Google Fonts (recommend Vercel).

Task ID: 4
Agent: Claude (chat)
Task: Add a history "Import" feature (mirroring the JSON export format) and improve currency-converter reliability (fully offline fallback) and amount formatting (locale thousand separators, per-currency decimal caps, float-artifact cleanup) — without changing the visual identity, calculator logic, or any working feature.

Work Log:
- Read `worklog.md` in full plus every file the task touches (`src/hooks/useHistory.ts`, `src/lib/exportHistory.ts`, `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx`, `src/components/calculator/Calculator.tsx`, `src/app/api/currency/route.ts`, `src/lib/converters.ts`, `src/components/calculator/Converter.tsx`, `src/lib/currencyData.ts`) to confirm the existing export JSON shape (`{ app, exportedAt, count, items: [{ expression, result, label, timestamp: ISOString }] }`) and existing `.calc-export-btn`/`.calc-export-item` styling before writing any import code.

Task A — Import History:
- Extended `src/hooks/useHistory.ts`: added an exported `ImportableHistoryItem` type and a new `addMany(incoming)` store action. It builds a `Set` of `expression\u0000result\u0000timestamp` keys from the existing items (and from items already queued in the same batch) to dedupe, merges new items with the existing list sorted newest-first, slices to the existing `MAX_ITEMS` (100) cap — so the oldest entries are always the ones dropped — and returns the count of items that actually ended up persisted (post-dedupe *and* post-cap, which is the number that matters for the confirmation toast). Exposed `addMany` from the hook's return value.
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/Calculator.tsx` to pass `onImport={history.addMany}` into `HistoryPanel`.
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx`:
  - Added a new `parseImportPayload(text)` + `normalizeImportRow(raw)` pair: `JSON.parse`s the file, verifies the payload is an object with an `items` array (throws a clear, user-facing message otherwise), then maps/filters each row — requiring non-empty string `expression`/`result`, defaulting `label` to `""` (capped at 80 chars, matching `updateLabel`'s existing limit), and coercing `timestamp` (accepts a `number`, an ISO string via `Date.parse`, or falls back to `Date.now()` for anything else) — so malformed files degrade gracefully instead of crashing.
  - Added an "Import" button (reusing the existing `.calc-export-btn` class so it matches the Download button pixel-for-pixel) plus a hidden `<input type="file" accept=".json,application/json">` it triggers. Moved this into the top of `.calc-history-actions` so it always sits directly next to Download — restructured that row so Import is always rendered (useful even with zero history) while the Download dropdown/Clear-all button remain conditional on `items.length > 0`, exactly as before.
  - `handleImportFile` reads the file via `file.text()`, parses/validates it, calls `onImport`, and shows a themed toast (`useToast`, `className: "calc-toast"`, matching the exact pattern already used for copy-to-clipboard in `useCalculator.ts`) reporting how many items were added — or that everything in the file was already present. Parse/validation failures are shown as an inline error line (rose-tinted, same visual language as the existing divide-by-zero error chip in `Display.tsx`) rather than crashing; the file input is reset after every selection so re-importing the same file re-fires the change handler.

Task B — Currency Reliability & Formatting:
- Created `src/lib/offlineRates.ts` — a static, clearly-labeled (`OFFLINE_RATES_DATE_LABEL = "offline snapshot — may be outdated"`) table of approximate USD rates for ~95 currencies covering every region in `currencyData.ts`, baked into the bundle as a last-resort fallback.
- Rewrote `src/app/api/currency/route.ts`: added a `source: "primary" | "fallback" | "offline"` field to `RatesResponse`, tagged `fetchPrimary`/`fetchFallback` accordingly, and added a new `offlineFallback()` function that can never throw. `GET` now tries primary → catches to fallback → catches to `offlineFallback()`, so the route always returns `200` with usable rates instead of ever surfacing a `502`. Offline responses are cached for only 5 minutes (vs. the normal 1 hour) so the route retries the live sources again soon after connectivity returns, rather than being stuck showing stale offline data for a full hour.
- Extended `src/lib/converters.ts`'s `formatConverted` with a new **optional** second `currencyCode` parameter — fully backward compatible, so the existing 1-arg call in `UnitConverter` needed no changes. When a currency code is passed, it rounds through `toPrecision(12)` first (killing float noise like `12.000000004`) then formats via `toLocaleString` with a decimal cap of 0 for JPY/KRW-style currencies (added a `ZERO_DECIMAL_CURRENCIES` set) and 2 for everything else. Without a currency code (unit conversions), it still cleans float artifacts via the existing `formatResult` and now additionally adds locale thousand separators via a small `addThousandSeparators` helper.
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/Converter.tsx`: `CurrencyConverter` now passes the target currency code into `formatConverted(value, to)`; added a `source` field to the local `CurrencyRates` type and a `.calc-offline-badge` pill (new `WifiOff` icon) that renders under the result whenever `rates.source === "offline"`, with the meta line also swapping to "· offline estimate" instead of showing a fabricated live-rate date.
- Caught a real regression risk while adding thousand separators: `UnitConverter`'s `swap()` reuses the currently-displayed `result` string as the next input value. Since `formatConverted` can now return e.g. `"1,234,567.89"`, reusing it verbatim would have broken `Number.parseFloat` on the next render (stops at the first comma). Fixed by stripping commas (`result.replace(/,/g, "")`) before feeding it back into `setValue` — the visual output is unaffected, only the internal reuse path.
- Added `.calc-offline-badge` styling to `src/app/globals.css`, next to the existing `.calc-conv-meta` rule, using the same amber/gold-adjacent warning tone as the rest of the premium theme (not the rose error color, since this is informational rather than an error).

Verification & Fixes:
- `npm install` failed in this sandbox: the egress proxy returned `403 host_not_allowed` for `registry.npmjs.org` on every package (even after 10+ retries across several minutes, and after temporarily stripping `@mdxeditor/editor` + regenerating the lockfile to rule out a single bad package) — no `node_modules` could be installed, so a real `npx tsc --noEmit` / `npx eslint .` run against the full dependency graph was not possible here. This mirrors the Google Fonts network restriction noted in Task 3's worklog entry; recommend running `npx tsc --noEmit && npx eslint .` once in an environment with normal npm registry access (e.g. locally or on Vercel) as a final gate before merging.
- As a substitute, ran a dependency-free syntax pass with a globally-available `tsc` (v6.0.3) across every changed/added file (`--noEmit --jsx react-jsx --skipLibCheck --strict false`, filtering out expected "cannot find module" errors from the missing `node_modules`): zero `TS1xxx` (syntax) errors in any file. Also ran a brace/paren balance check across all seven changed files — all balanced.
- Manually traced the import pipeline in Node against a hand-built sample export file (matching `exportHistoryJson`'s real shape, including ISO-string timestamps): `normalizeImportRow` correctly coerces every field; verified `addMany`'s dedupe against three scenarios — (1) an item identical to an existing one is skipped and the toast would report 0 new; (2) importing 5 very old items on top of 99 existing newer ones correctly keeps only 100 total and evicts the older imported items first (cap always drops the oldest, confirmed by timestamp); (3) two identical rows within the same imported file collapse to one. All three matched expectations.
- Manually traced the currency route's fallback chain in Node with mocked fetches: primary-up → `source: "primary"`; primary-down/fallback-up → `source: "fallback"`; both down → `source: "offline"` with the baked-in table — confirming the route can no longer return a `502` and that `Converter.tsx`'s `rates.source === "offline"` check (which drives the badge) fires at exactly the right point.
- Manually verified `formatConverted`'s new behavior in Node: `0.1 + 0.2` formatted as a PKR amount → `"0.30"` (no float noise); `12.000000004` as USD → `"12.00"`; a large PKR amount → `"1,234,567.89"`; a JPY amount → zero-decimal `"1,235"`; a large unit-conversion result (no currency code) → `"1,000,000"` with separators; a tiny unit result → `"0.000001"` unaffected. Also confirmed the `UnitConverter` swap fix: stripping commas from a separator-formatted result before feeding it back into the amount field re-parses correctly with `Number.parseFloat`.
- Existing `src/lib/__tests__/converters.test.ts` only exercises `convertUnit` (not `formatConverted`), so it's unaffected by this task's formatting changes; it couldn't be re-run here regardless since `bun`/`node_modules` weren't available in this sandbox for the same network reason as above.

Stage Summary:
- History can now be imported from a previously-exported JSON file via a new "Import" button sitting directly beside "Download" in the history panel, with clear inline errors for malformed files, dedupe-safe merging (by expression+result+timestamp), respect for the existing 100-item cap (oldest-first eviction), and a themed toast confirming how many items were added.
- The currency converter is now resilient to total network loss: primary (open.er-api.com) → fallback (frankfurter.app) → a new fully offline, clearly-labeled static rate table, with a visible "Offline / approximate rates" badge whenever that last resort is in use. The route no longer returns a 502 under any failure combination.
- Currency and unit conversion amounts now use locale-aware thousand separators and clean up floating-point artifacts (e.g. `12.000000004` → `12.00`); currency amounts additionally cap decimals per currency (0dp for JPY/KRW-style currencies, 2dp otherwise). `formatConverted`'s existing single-argument signature is fully preserved (the currency code is an optional second parameter), so no other caller needed to change.
- Caught and fixed a regression the formatting change would otherwise have introduced: `UnitConverter`'s swap button now strips thousand separators before reusing a formatted result as the next input value, so it still re-parses correctly.
- `npm install`/`npx tsc`/`npx eslint` could not be run against the real dependency graph in this sandbox due to `registry.npmjs.org` being blocked by the egress proxy for the full session (not a transient blip — confirmed via 10+ retries and direct `curl`). Substituted a dependency-free `tsc` syntax pass (clean, zero `TS1xxx` errors) and hand-traced/simulated every piece of new logic (import dedupe/cap, currency fallback chain, formatting output, swap fix) in Node against realistic inputs. Recommend a final `npx tsc --noEmit && npx eslint .` pass in an environment with normal registry access before merging.

Rows alternate between two navy shades (`PDF_THEME.cardA`/`cardB`, both used elsewhere in the theme) instead of the previous flat light-gray banding; expression text uses `--c-text`, results use the gold `--c-result-1` tone in bold, labels use `--c-accent-soft` italic, and timestamps use `--c-text-muted`.
  - Added a second pass after all pages/rows are drawn: `doc.getNumberOfPages()` gives the true total, then loops `doc.setPage(p)` for every page to draw a thin gold-alpha footer divider plus "Ahmed Premium Calculator" (left) and "Page X of Y" (right) — identical placement on every page, and correct even when the row loop added pages mid-stream (the count wasn't knowable until after the fact).

PDF_THEME.cardA : PDF_THEME.cardB))` failed TS2556 because a ternary between two readonly tuples isn't inferred as a tuple for spreading — fixed by binding the chosen tuple to a `const` first and passing its three elements explicitly; (2) `doc.internal.getNumberOfPages()` doesn't exist on jsPDF's `internal` type — `getNumberOfPages()` lives directly on the `jsPDF` instance, fixed the call site accordingly.

  - `HistoryPanel.tsx` — added `aria-label`s to the Import button and the Clear-all button (previously text-only), and to the memory-adjacent Download trigger.
  - Verified via a real rendered page (`curl` output of `next dev`'s HTML, parsed with a small script) that all 44 `<button>` elements and every `<select>`/`<input>` in the tree now resolve to a non-empty accessible name — zero remaining gaps.
- **Accessibility — keyboard-unreachable control (real bug, not just missing labels):** `HistoryPanel.tsx`'s history-item body (`.calc-history-body`, the clickable area that reuses a past calculation) was `role="button"` with `tabIndex={-1}` and no `onKeyDown` — meaning it could never be reached via Tab or activated via Enter/Space, only by mouse/touch click. Changed `tabIndex` to `0`, added an `onKeyDown` handler firing `onReuse` on Enter/Space, and added a descriptive `aria-label` (`"Reuse calculation: {expression} equals {result}"`) so the accessible name doesn't just read as "button".
- **Mobile responsiveness (375px) fixes** — reasoned through and fixed by tracing the actual CSS box model rather than guessing, since no persistent browser session was available in this sandbox (see Verification section):
  - **CurrencySelect dropdown (the real bug in scope):** in the currency "From" row, `CurrencySelect` shares a `grid-template-columns: 1fr auto 1fr` row with the amount input and swap button, so its own trigger column is only ~130px wide at 375px viewport width. `.calc-csel-panel` was `left: 0; right: 0` — pinned to that same narrow column — so the searchable dropdown itself was squeezed to ~130px, making currency names hard to read/tap even though nothing technically overflowed. Fixed by anchoring the panel from `right: 0` and giving it `width: max(100%, 240px)` with `max-width: calc(100vw - 32px)` as a hard viewport safety cap — it now floats wide enough to be usable while never overflowing the screen, and is unchanged (still exactly 100% width) for the "To" row where the container is already full-width.
  - Added `min-width: 0` to `.calc-csel`, `.calc-select`, `.calc-amount`, and changed `.calc-conv-row`'s grid columns to `minmax(0, 1fr) auto minmax(0, 1fr)` — without this, CSS Grid's implicit `min-width: auto` on grid items can force a track wider than its share of the row, which is a common invisible cause of horizontal overflow on narrow screens even when nothing "looks" wrong in a quick check.
  - **History controls:** `.calc-history-del` (the per-item delete "×") was `opacity: 0` by default and only `opacity: 1` on `:hover` — invisible and effectively undiscoverable on any touch device, since touchscreens have no hover state. Added `@media (hover: none) { .calc-history-del { opacity: 0.55; } }` so it's always visibly present (if a bit understated) on touch, plus `:focus-visible` reveals it for keyboard users, and a `:active` press-scale for tactile feedback.
  - **Download menu / Import menu:** added `max-width: calc(100vw - 32px)` to `.calc-export-dropdown` as the same defensive viewport cap (it already fit comfortably at 375px given `.calc-history-panel`'s `min(360px, 92vw)` width and the dropdown's 160px min-width, but this removes any edge-case risk on sub-360px devices).
  - Manually re-derived the box model for the history/settings slide-out panels, the topbar (tabs + 5 utility icons), and the keypad grid at a 375px viewport width and confirmed every element still fits without clipping; the rounded `28px` calculator card radius is untouched and nothing pierces it, since dropdowns/panels are positioned outside the card's own box rather than clipped by it (the card has no `overflow: hidden` and never did).
- **Console warnings:** audited every component for the usual dev-mode culprits — unstable `key`s, `setState` calls during render, effects with missing/incorrect dependencies, uncontrolled↔controlled input switches — and found none introduced by or present in the calculator components. Confirmed via a live `next dev` run (see Verification) that the only warnings emitted are pre-existing, out-of-scope Google Fonts network warnings (`next/font` falling back because `fonts.googleapis.com` is blocked by this sandbox's egress proxy — same limitation noted in Task 3/4's worklog entries) and two pre-existing `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect` ESLint errors in `src/components/ui/carousel.tsx` and `src/hooks/use-mobile.ts`, both outside this task's scope (`src/components/calculator/*` / `globals.css`) and explicitly called out as ignorable in this task's instructions.
- **Micro-interactions added** (kept deliberately restrained per the "do not over-animate" instruction):
  - **Successful export flash:** clicking any Download-menu format (CSV/Excel/JSON/TXT/PDF) now briefly swaps the Download button's icon to a checkmark and plays a 1.1s gold pulse (`calc-flash-success` / `@keyframes calc-flash-pulse`) before reverting — for the two async formats (Excel, PDF) the flash only fires after the export promise actually resolves, not optimistically on click.
  - **Successful import flash:** the same checkmark + gold-pulse treatment fires on the Import button after a successful import (i.e. when at least one new item was actually added), alongside the existing toast — kept silent (no flash) when the import found nothing new to add, so the visual doesn't imply success on a no-op.
  - **Consistent gold-glow press feedback:** several secondary controls (`.calc-util-btn`, `.calc-export-btn`, `.calc-history-clear`, `.calc-csel-trigger`, `.calc-history-del`) previously had hover states but no `:active` press feedback at all, unlike `CalculatorButton`'s ripple + scale. Added matching `:active { transform: translateY(1px) scale(0.94-0.98) }` (plus a soft gold ring on the utility icons) so pressing any control in the app feels consistent with the keypad — without adding new ripple DOM nodes or JS, keeping this lightweight.
  - Deliberately did **not** touch `CalculatorButton.tsx`'s existing ripple (already correct and explicitly called out as "don't break") and did not add new animated elements to the Display/Keypad/ScientificKeypad, which were already appropriately quiet.
- **Small UI inconsistencies checked and confirmed already consistent (no change needed):** icon+text gap spacing across `.calc-export-btn`/`.calc-history-clear`/`.calc-mem-btn`; button corner radii; the 4-column keypad grid gap; the topbar's flex-wrap behavior under 460px (already had a dedicated media query from Phase 2). Only the CSS listed above needed real changes; the rest of the "spacing/alignment/padding/margins/icon alignment" surface was already solid from prior tasks.

Verification & Fixes:
- `npm install` succeeded in this session (869 packages, same as Task 5's environment — `registry.npmjs.org` was reachable here). Ran `npx tsc --noEmit` and captured the output *before* making any changes as a baseline: 6 pre-existing errors, all in `examples/websocket/*` (missing `socket.io`/`socket.io-client` types) and `src/lib/__tests__/*` (missing `bun:test` types) — none in scope. - **New master asset processing** (`/home/claude/work/gen_assets.py` + `gen2.py`/`gen3.py`, run locally with Pillow — this sandbox's `bash_tool` had npm registry access this session, but the icon art itself is still raster-sourced rather than `sharp`/SVG-rendered): loaded the supplied 1254×1254 medallion and recolored every near-black pixel (`max(r,g,b) < 18`) to the app's exact navy token `#0a0e17`, matching the approach Task 7A used on the lower-res master — gives a crisper source for every downstream resize than the old 640px asset.

- **Refreshed existing assets from the crisper master**: re-rendered `public/agc-mark.png` (160×160 navbar/Settings mark) and `public/agc-logo.png` (640×640 About-panel hero) from the new 1254px source for a sharper result than Task 7A's 640px-sourced versions; `icon-192.png`, `icon-512.png`, and `icon-maskable-512.png` were likewise regenerated in place (same filenames, crisper art).

- **`public/sw.js`**: bumped the cache key to `agc-calc-v2` (so the existing activate-step cache-cleanup logic evicts the old `v1` cache holding stale icon bytes on the next visit) and expanded `APP_SHELL` to precache `favicon.ico`, the 192/512 "any" icons, both maskable icons, and the Apple touch icon — so the install/offline experience has fresh branding immediately rather than only after a second fetch.
- **Splash screen — two distinct things this task's brief covers**:
  1. **iOS PWA launch screens** (the nine `apple-touch-startup-image` PNGs above): built with Pillow — a soft radial navy-to-navy-deep gradient background matching the app shell's own ambient-glow look, a blurred gold halo behind the medallion, and the medallion centered at ~34% of the shorter viewport dimension. These are what iOS actually displays for a split second on cold-launch from the home screen before the page paints, replacing the plain white flash Safari shows by default when no startup images are declared.
  2. **In-app animated boot splash** (new `src/components/calculator/SplashScreen.tsx`, mounted at the top of `src/app/page.tsx`): a full-viewport overlay shown on first mount — the AGC mark scales+fades in (`cubic-bezier(0.16,1,0.3,1)`, matching the "premium ease" curve already used elsewhere in the app) inside two staggered expanding gold rings, "AGC" and "Building Digital Excellence" fade up beneath it, and a thin gold shimmer bar sweeps once — then after a short hold the whole overlay fades+scales out and the component unmounts (removed from the DOM, not just hidden, so it never intercepts clicks or gets left in the accessibility tree). Wraps the timing in `prefers-reduced-motion` handling (shorter hold, `animation-duration: 0.01ms` override on every splash keyframe) per the app's existing accessibility bar. All colors/fonts pull from the same `--c-*` theme tokens and `--font-space-grotesk` variable as the rest of the app, so it re-skins correctly across all four themes without any new hardcoded colors.
- **`scripts/icon.svg`** and **`public/logo.svg`** were deliberately left as Task 7A wrote them (simplified vector "AGC-in-a-ring" glyphs, not a true vectorization of the raster medallion) — the actual medallion is photoreal raster art with gradients/bevels that isn't reasonably reproducible as flat-fill SVG, and the existing vector files still serve their two real purposes (a future `sharp`-based `gen-icons.ts` regeneration path, and the visual reference `exportHistory.ts`'s PDF-export logo-drawing code cites in a comment) unchanged.

Task ID: 7C
Agent: main (Z.ai Code orchestrator)
Task: Upgrade the PDF export — add the real AGC logo in the header, an AGC watermark on every page, a premium branded background, footer branding, and "Page X of Y" — without breaking pagination or text wrapping.

Work Log:
- Read `worklog.md` in full (Tasks 1–7B), then re-read `src/lib/exportHistory.ts` end-to-end (Task 5's PDF redesign plus Task 7A's later text-only rebrand) to confirm exactly what already existed before changing anything: a vector-drawn logo mark (`drawLogoMark`), a flat navy `PDF_THEME.bg` page fill, a branded header/summary/table already repeated per page via `startNewPage()`, and a footer that already printed "AGC Premium Calculator" + "Page X of Y" on every page (from Task 5) — so this task's real gaps were a **raster** logo, an actual **watermark**, and a **premium** (non-flat) background; "Page X of Y" and basic footer branding already existed and only needed extending, not adding from scratch.
- Confirmed only `exportHistoryPdf` (and its private helpers) needed to change — `exportHistoryCsv`/`Txt`/`Json`/`Xlsx` and the shared `historyRows()` helper were read but left untouched, matching this task's scope.
- **Real AGC logo in the header** — added `loadImageDataUrl(path)`, a small helper that `fetch`s a `public/` asset and resolves it to a base64 data URL via `FileReader`, resolving to `null` on any failure (offline, blocked fetch, decode error) rather than throwing, so the export can never fail just because an image didn't load. `exportHistoryPdf` now loads `/agc-mark.png` (crisp small icon, used in the header and footer) and `/agc-logo.png` (the larger hero medallion, used for the watermark) once, in parallel, before generating any page. `drawBrandHeader` now takes the loaded mark data URL and, when present, draws the real medallion via `doc.addImage()` inside the exact same gold-ringed rounded-square frame the old vector mark used (identical position/size), so the header's layout is pixel-for-pixel unchanged either way; the original `drawLogoMark()` vector routine is kept and used automatically as the fallback if the fetch/decode failed.
- **AGC watermark on every page** — new `drawWatermark()`: draws the large hero logo centered on the page at very low opacity (jsPDF `GState`/`opacity` API, wrapped in try/catch) *plus* a large, rotated, low-contrast "AGC" wordmark layered in the same spot, so there's always a visible watermark even in a jsPDF build without the opacity plugin. Guarded so the raster image is only ever drawn when the opacity call actually succeeded — if `GState` isn't available, the code skips the image (rather than risk it rendering at full strength over the table) and relies solely on the low-contrast text fallback. Called once per page inside `paintPageBackground()`, before the header/table/rows are drawn, so it always sits behind real content and never reduces legibility.
- **Premium branded background** — new `drawPremiumBackdrop()`, replacing the previous single flat `PDF_THEME.bg` rectangle: a soft multi-band vertical shading (interpolated between `bgDeep`/`bg` in a triangle wave, lightest at page-center) approximating a subtle vignette since jsPDF has no native gradient fill, plus a thin double gold frame inset from the page edge (echoing the app's own bordered glass-card language) with small gold diamond corner accents at all four corners, nodding to the medallion's own "· BUILDING DIGITAL EXCELLENCE ·" diamond motif. Drawn on every page immediately after the flat navy fill and before the watermark.
- **Footer branding** — extended (not replaced) the existing footer loop: added the small raster AGC mark as a footer icon next to the brand name, and a second line ("Ahmed Group of Companies · Building Digital Excellence") beneath "AGC Premium Calculator", with "Page X of Y" kept exactly where it was (right-aligned, same baseline as the brand name). Grew `footerHeight` from 34pt to 50pt to fit the extra line cleanly above the new decorative frame border (re-verified the added 16pt doesn't cause any row to overflow past the footer — the page-break check already compares against `pageHeight - footerHeight`, so it automatically became slightly more conservative, not less).
- Left `exportHistoryPdf`'s function signature (`(items: HistoryItem[]) => Promise<void>`), output filename (`agc-calculator-history.pdf`), the summary strip, the table column layout/wrapping logic, and the page-break-before-drawing pagination rule completely untouched — every change is additive drawing calls layered around the existing, already-verified row/column logic.

Verification & Fixes:
- This sandbox session had no `registry.npmjs.org` access (`403 host_not_allowed`) and no pre-existing `node_modules`, so a real `npm install` / `npx tsc --noEmit` / `npx eslint .` run (as prior PDF-touching tasks 5 and 7A/7B were able to do) wasn't possible here. Used the same fallback prior tasks have used when network was unavailable: a globally available standalone `typescript` (v6.0.3) run against the changed file in isolation (`tsc --noEmit --skipLibCheck --strict false`) — the only errors reported are the expected "cannot find module" noise for `@/lib/calculator`, `@/hooks/useHistory`, `xlsx`, and `jspdf` (all real dependencies that simply aren't installed in this session), with zero actual syntax or type errors in the changed code itself. Also ran a Node brace/paren-balance check across the full file (both balanced).
- Manually re-traced the full render order for both the first page and every subsequent page (`startNewPage()`) to confirm draw layering is correct: flat navy fill → premium backdrop (shading + frame + corner ticks) → watermark (opacity-guarded logo + faint rotated "AGC" text) → opaque header band → (summary, first page only) → table column header → rows, with the footer drawn last in a second pass over every page once the true page count is known — confirming the watermark and backdrop always sit behind real content and the header/footer never get overdrawn by anything added in this task.
- Specifically re-checked the pagination-safety guarantees this task was told not to break: the row-height pre-check (`if (y + rowHeight > pageHeight - footerHeight)`) still fires before any row is drawn, `doc.splitTextToSize()` still measures wrapped line counts across all three columns before computing row height, and `startNewPage()` still repaints the full background/header/table-header on every new page exactly as before — the only numeric change relevant to pagination is `footerHeight` growing from 34 to 50, which only makes the existing page-break check slightly more conservative (breaks a hair earlier to protect the taller footer), never less safe.
- Traced the opacity fallback path explicitly since it can't be verified without a live jsPDF build in this session: if `new doc.GState({ opacity: … })` / `doc.setGState()` throw (caught via `unknown`-typed casts, not `any`, matching the project's existing type-safety style elsewhere in this file), `drawWatermark()` skips the raster logo entirely and falls back to a low-contrast (near-background-color) "AGC" text watermark instead of ever risking a full-opacity image drowning out the table — confirmed this branch by temporarily forcing `applyFaintOpacity()` to return `false` in a scratch copy of the function and reading through the resulting draw calls by hand.
- Confirmed via `grep` that `historyRows()`, `exportHistoryCsv`, `exportHistoryTxt`, `exportHistoryJson`, and `exportHistoryXlsx` are byte-identical to before this task, and that `HistoryPanel.tsx`'s call site (`exportHistoryPdf(items)`) didn't need any change since the function's signature and behavior contract (async, void, same filename) are unchanged.
- Diffed the project tree against the Task 7B upload (`diff -rq`, excluding `node_modules`/`.next`/build artifacts): confirmed exactly one file changed — `src/lib/exportHistory.ts` — and nothing else in the project (every component, every other lib file, all icon/splash assets from 7B) was touched.

Stage Summary:
- `exportHistoryPdf()`'s report now carries the real AGC gold-phoenix medallion instead of only a flat vector glyph: the actual raster logo in the header (with the original vector mark kept as an automatic fallback if the image can't load), a faint centered AGC watermark (logo + rotated wordmark) on every page, a premium shaded-and-framed background replacing the old flat navy fill, and a fuller footer (brand icon + "Ahmed Group of Companies · Building Digital Excellence" tagline) alongside the "Page X of Y" counter that already existed from Task 5.
- Every new draw call is layered strictly behind or after existing content in the same order the report already used, so pagination (page-break-before-drawing row heights, multi-line wrap measurement, repeated header/table-header on new pages) and the existing summary/table/row rendering are unchanged and unbroken.
- `npx tsc --noEmit` / `npx eslint .` could not be run against the real dependency graph this session because this sandbox had no network access to `registry.npmjs.org` (`403 host_not_allowed`) and no pre-existing `node_modules` to reuse; used the same globally-available-`tsc` syntax/type fallback prior sessions have used under identical network constraints, which reported zero errors introduced by this change (only expected missing-module noise for real, uninstalled dependencies). This should be re-verified with a real `npm install` + `npx tsc --noEmit` + `npx eslint .` in an environment with registry access before merging, exactly as the task instructions requested.

Task ID: 7D
Agent: Claude (chat)
Task: Brand every exported file format — Excel (AGC logo, company name, gold title, navy headers), DOCX (AGC logo, header, footer), and CSV/TXT/JSON (company metadata before the exported data) — without breaking pagination, existing formats, or any other feature. Verify with `npx tsc --noEmit` and `npx eslint .`.

Work Log:
- Read `worklog.md` in full (Tasks 1–7C) before touching anything, then read `src/lib/exportHistory.ts` end-to-end to confirm exactly what already existed: the PDF export (Task 5 + 7C) was already fully branded (raster logo, watermark, premium background, branded footer, "Page X of Y") and out of scope here; CSV/TXT/JSON/XLSX were still on their original Task 1–3 implementations — TXT already had a basic "AGC PREMIUM CALCULATOR" header line, but CSV had no metadata at all, JSON's metadata was a single `app` field, and Excel (via plain SheetJS) had no styling/branding capability whatsoever (the free `xlsx`/SheetJS build the project depended on cannot write cell fills, fonts, or embedded images — confirmed by inspecting `node_modules/xlsx`'s write path before deciding on a library change). Also confirmed via `grep` that **no DOCX export existed anywhere in the project** — the task's "DOCX" requirement meant adding this format from scratch, not re-branding an existing one.
- Confirmed this sandbox session had live `registry.npmjs.org` access (`npm view exceljs version` / `npm view docx version` both resolved), so real packages could be installed and verified for real rather than falling back to a syntax-only pass.
- **Library choice**: swapped the Excel export from `xlsx` (SheetJS Community Edition, no styling/image support) to `exceljs@4.4.0`, which supports cell fills, fonts, and embedded images — the only way to satisfy "AGC logo / gold title / navy headers" for real. Added `docx@9.7.1` (Header/Footer/ImageRun/Table shading support, works in-browser via dynamic import) since no Word export previously existed. Removed the now-unused `xlsx` package from `package.json` after confirming (via `grep -rn` across `src/`) nothing else in the project imported it.
- Added a shared `BRAND` constant (`app`, `company`, `tagline`) and a shared `BRAND_HEX` palette (navy/navyDeep/gold/goldBright/text/textMuted, matching the existing PDF theme's `--c-*`-derived tones) at the top of `exportHistory.ts` so every format pulls from one source of truth instead of repeating literal brand strings/colors.
- **CSV** (`exportHistoryCsv`): now prepends a company-metadata block ahead of the real header/data — app name, `"{company} — {tagline}"`, export timestamp, and total-record count, followed by a blank row — before the existing `Expression,Result,Label,Timestamp` header and rows. Kept the exact same column shape/escaping/filename as before, so nothing that reads the data rows (there is no CSV-import feature) is affected.
- **TXT** (`exportHistoryTxt`): extended the existing header block to also include the `"{company} · {tagline}"` line and a `Total Records:` count line, sourced from the new shared `BRAND` constant instead of a hardcoded literal.
- **JSON** (`exportHistoryJson`): added `company` and `tagline` fields to the existing top-level payload (alongside the pre-existing `app`/`exportedAt`/`count`/`items`) — confirmed safe against the existing Import feature by re-reading `HistoryPanel.tsx`'s `parseImportPayload`, which only requires an `items` array and ignores/permits any other top-level fields, so this is fully backward- and forward-compatible with previously exported files.
- **Excel** (`exportHistoryXlsx`, rewritten on `exceljs`): builds a `"Calculation History"` worksheet (named worksheets called literally `"History"` are a *reserved* name in ExcelJS/Excel — caught this as a real bug during verification, see below) with: the real AGC mark (`/agc-mark.png`, loaded via the existing `loadImageDataUrl` helper) embedded top-left over a 4-column-wide navy (`#060912`) brand band; a gold (`#F0D378`) bold title row (`"AGC PREMIUM CALCULATOR"`); a company/tagline subtitle row; an export-meta/record-count row; then a navy-filled (`#0A0E17`), gold-text (`#D4AF37`), bold table header row (`Expression / Result / Label / Timestamp`) with a gold bottom border; data rows with subtle alternating row banding and bold gold-toned result cells; frozen header pane (`ySplit: 7`) so the header stays visible on scroll; falls back gracefully (no image, tighter cell indent) if the logo can't be loaded. Same output filename (`agc-calculator-history.xlsx`) and function signature as before.
- **Word/DOCX** (`exportHistoryDocx`, new): built with the `docx` library — a running **Header** (real AGC mark + `"AGC Premium Calculator · Calculation History Report"`) and running **Footer** (`"{company} · {tagline} — Page {PageNumber.CURRENT} of {PageNumber.TOTAL_PAGES}"`, using `docx`'s built-in page-number fields so it stays correct across however many pages Word itself paginates the table into) repeated on every page automatically by Word's own header/footer mechanism; a navy-banded gold title block, company/tagline line, report subtitle, and export-meta/count line in the body; then a `Table` whose header row uses navy cell shading + bold gold text (mirroring the Excel/PDF treatment) and whose data rows alternate a soft cream shading, with gold-toned bold result cells and muted timestamp cells. Added `loadImageArrayBuffer()` (a sibling to the existing `loadImageDataUrl`) since `docx`'s `ImageRun` wants raw image bytes rather than a data-URL string. New output filename `agc-calculator-history.docx`; function signature matches the other async export functions (`(items: HistoryItem[]) => Promise<void>`).
- Added a type-only import (`import type { Paragraph as DocxParagraph, Table as DocxTable, TableRow as DocxTableRow } from "docx"`) to type the DOCX builder's intermediate arrays — destructuring `Paragraph`/`Table`/`TableRow` only as *values* from the dynamic `await import("docx")` doesn't give TypeScript a usable *type* for annotations, so a separate type-only import was needed alongside the runtime dynamic import (the dynamic import itself is still what actually loads the library code — this was purely a type-checking fix, verified by the `tsc` diff below).
- Rewired `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx`: imported the new `exportHistoryDocx` and a `FileType` icon (lucide-react), and added a "Word (.docx)" item to the existing Download dropdown, positioned right after "Excel (.xlsx)" — follows the exact same async-export-then-flash pattern already used for Excel/PDF (`.then(() => flashExport("docx")).catch(() => {})`), so the existing success-flash micro-interaction (Task 6) works for the new format with no other changes.
- Left `exportHistoryPdf` (Task 5 + 7C's already-fully-branded report), `historyRows()`, and every other component/hook/lib file completely untouched — confirmed via a full-tree diff against the Task 7C upload at the end of this task (see Verification).

Verification & Fixes:
- This session had live npm registry access, so `npm install exceljs@4.4.0 docx@9.7.1 --save` (971 packages) succeeded for real, enabling genuine `tsc`/`eslint` runs and genuine library behavior — not a syntax-only substitute.
- Captured a pre-change baseline exactly as prior tasks have done: `npx tsc --noEmit` → the same 6 pre-existing/out-of-scope errors (`examples/websocket/*` missing `socket.io` types, `src/lib/__tests__/*` missing `bun:test` types); `npx eslint .` → the same 2 pre-existing `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect` errors in `carousel.tsx`/`use-mobile.ts`. After every change (including the final `xlsx`-removal cleanup), re-ran both and diffed byte-for-byte against this baseline: **identical in both cases** — zero new errors introduced by this task, in either the intermediate or final state.
- Built a throwaway Node/`tsx` verification harness (not part of the delivered app; installed `tsx` as a dev dependency, used it, then fully uninstalled it and deleted the harness file before packaging) that shimmed just enough of the browser environment — `fetch` (serving real files straight from `public/`), a `FileReader` polyfill (Node has none; this is what real browsers provide, so its absence here is a test-harness gap, not an app bug), and `document`/`URL.createObjectURL` to capture each export's `Blob` to disk — then called every export function with realistic multi-item history data (including a long label/expression to check wrapping) and wrote the real output bytes for inspection:
  - **CSV/TXT/JSON**: inspected the written files directly — confirmed the new metadata lines/fields appear exactly as designed ahead of the real data, and that the existing per-row data (expression/result/label/ISO timestamp) is unchanged.
  - **Excel**: first run failed immediately with `Error: The name "History" is protected. Please use a different name.` — a real bug caught during verification (ExcelJS reserves the literal sheet name `"History"` for Excel's own change-tracking feature). Fixed by renaming the sheet to `"Calculation History"`, re-ran, and it now writes cleanly. Second issue also caught: the AGC mark wasn't actually being embedded on the first run (`ws._images` empty when re-opened with `openpyxl`, and the xlsx's zip had no `xl/media`/`xl/drawings` at all) — traced this to the *test harness* lacking a `FileReader` shim (which `loadImageDataUrl` depends on and which only exists in real browsers), not an app bug; added the shim, re-ran, and confirmed via direct zip inspection that `xl/media/image1.png` and `xl/drawings/drawing1.xml` are now present (file size grew from 7.4 KB to 47 KB, consistent with the embedded PNG). Also opened the workbook with `openpyxl` and confirmed programmatically: title cell (`"AGC PREMIUM CALCULATOR"`) has navy fill (`FF060912`) + gold-bright text (`FFF0D378`); the table header row has navy fill (`FF0A0E17`) + gold text (`FFD4AF37`); frozen-pane view is set; all four data columns populated correctly.
  - **Word**: unzipped the generated `.docx` and confirmed structurally — `word/header1.xml` and `word/footer1.xml` both exist (a running header/footer on every page, per Word's own section mechanism) and the header's XML references the embedded PNG relationship; `word/media/` contains the AGC mark; the footer XML contains both a `PAGE` and a `NUMPAGES` field code (confirming `PageNumber.CURRENT`/`PageNumber.TOTAL_PAGES` compiled to real, page-count-aware Word fields rather than static text); extracted all `<w:t>` text runs from `word/document.xml` and confirmed the title/company/tagline/summary lines and all table cell values (expression/result/label/timestamp) are present and correct; counted 13 `w:shd` (shading) elements and confirmed both the navy (`0A0E17`) and gold (`D4AF37`) hex values appear in the document XML, confirming the header-row/body shading and text-color treatment actually made it into the OOXML rather than being silently dropped.
  - Re-ran the same harness a second time after removing the now-unused `xlsx` package from `package.json`, to confirm the cleanup itself didn't regress anything — CSV/TXT/JSON/Excel/Word all still produced correct output. (PDF's own `jsPDF.prototype.save()` isn't compatible with this lightweight harness — it needs the fuller browser-API monkeypatch Task 5's verification session used — but `exportHistoryPdf` wasn't touched by this task at all, so it wasn't re-verified here; it remains as browser-verified in Task 5/7C's worklog entries.)
  - Found and removed one stray artifact this verification process itself produced (`agc-calculator-history.pdf`, ~1.3 MB, written to the project root by an earlier interrupted harness run) before the final tree diff — confirmed via `diff -rq` against the Task 7C upload that the *only* real changes are `package.json`/`package-lock.json` (dependency swap), `src/lib/exportHistory.ts`, and `src/components/calculator/HistoryPanel.tsx`.
- Deleted the verification harness file and `tsx` dev dependency after use; confirmed `package.json`'s `dependencies` now list `docx` and `exceljs` and no longer list `xlsx`; confirmed no test artifacts (`verify-out*`, `dbg*.xlsx`, `*.mjs`/`*.mts` scratch files) remain anywhere in the tree.

By this point the app had been through six rebranding/polish passes (7A–7E) plus five feature phases (1–6) and was already extensively verified; this task's job was a genuinely fresh, whole-project audit rather than assuming prior passes caught everything, and to fix anything still found — including things previously logged as "pre-existing/out of scope" in earlier tasks, per this task's explicit instruction not to wave issues through.
- Checked network access first: this sandbox session's `bash_tool` had no egress (`curl https://registry.npmjs.org` → `403`), and no `node_modules` was present (excluded from every delivered archive as instructed) — so a real `npm install` + `npx tsc --noEmit` + `npx eslint .` + `npm run build` + `npm run dev` against the live dependency graph was not possible here, the same constraint hit repeatedly in Tasks 3/4/7A/7C/7E. Used the same fallback those sessions established: a standalone, globally-available `tsc` (v6.0.3, `--noEmit --skipLibCheck --strict false --ignoreConfig`) run across every `.ts`/`.tsx` file in `src/`, filtering out the well-established environment-only noise (missing-module errors for real, uninstalled dependencies; missing global `React`/JSX-runtime types since no `@types/react` is resolvable standalone) that appears identically across files this task didn't touch.
- That pass surfaced two categories of finding, both fixed:
  1. **A real, fixable TypeScript/project-config issue**: `tsconfig.json`'s `include` glob (`**/*.ts`, `**/*.tsx`) picks up `examples/websocket/{server,frontend}.ts`, which import `socket.io`/`socket.io-client` — packages that are *not* and shouldn't be a dependency of this calculator app (dead reference/scaffold code, confirmed via `grep` that nothing under `src/` imports from `examples/`). This has been logged as a "pre-existing, out-of-scope" `tsc` error in every prior task's worklog entry since Task 3, without ever actually being fixed. Fixed it for real this time: added `"examples"` to `tsconfig.json`'s `exclude` array (matching `eslint.config.mjs`, which already ignores `examples/**` — so `tsc` and `eslint` are now consistent). This removes the long-standing false "6 pre-existing errors" baseline everyone kept re-diffing against; a real `npx tsc --noEmit` run should now be clean of `examples/*` noise. (The `bun:test`-type errors in `src/lib/__tests__/*` were not a real bug — `bun-types` is already a listed devDependency; those errors only appeared because `node_modules` wasn't installed in the sandboxes that reported them, and resolve on a real `npm install`.)
  2. Two files with a genuine `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect` ESLint error, repeatedly flagged since Task 6's baseline and always deferred as "pre-existing/out of scope" because they sit outside `src/components/calculator/*`. Fixed both properly instead of leaving them:
     - `src/hooks/use-mobile.ts` — replaced the `useState` + `useEffect`-with-a-synchronous-`setIsMobile`-call pattern with `React.useSyncExternalStore` (subscribe to the `matchMedia` `change` event, snapshot `window.innerWidth < BREAKPOINT`, `false` on the server) — the same SSR-safe pattern `useHistory.ts` already established in Task 2 for an analogous problem. No behavior change (same breakpoint, same reactivity), just no more synchronous `setState` inside an effect body.
     - `src/components/ui/carousel.tsx` — the effect that wires up Embla's `select`/`reInit` listeners was also calling `onSelect(api)` synchronously on mount to seed the initial `canScrollPrev`/`canScrollNext` state. Deferred that seed call to `requestAnimationFrame(() => onSelect(api))` (with the frame cancelled in cleanup) so the state write happens on the next frame instead of synchronously inside the effect — imperceptible to any actual carousel usage (this component isn't even wired into the calculator app yet, but it's part of the shared `ui/` kit and should still be clean).
- **Full-project accessibility audit of the three slide-out panels** (History/Settings/About), reading each one end-to-end rather than trusting the prior tasks' "no changes needed" audits at face value — found a genuine, previously-unnoticed gap: none of the three `<aside>` panels had `role="dialog"` / `aria-modal`, and none of them closed on <kbd>Escape</kbd> (a real, common expectation for any slide-out/overlay panel, and a real accessibility gap per WAI-ARIA dialog pattern guidance). Fixed properly:
  - Added a small shared hook, `src/hooks/useEscapeToClose.ts` (`useEffect` + a `window` `keydown` listener that calls `onClose` on `Escape`, only registered while `open` is true), to avoid duplicating the same listener logic three times.
  - Wired it into `SettingsPanel.tsx`, `HistoryPanel.tsx`, and `AboutPanel.tsx`; added `role="dialog"` and `aria-modal={open}` to each panel's `<aside>` alongside the `aria-label` it already had.
  - **Caught a real interaction bug this fix would otherwise have introduced**: `useCalculator.ts`'s global keyboard handler already treats <kbd>Escape</kbd> as "clear the whole calculator" (`allClear()`), with no awareness of whether a panel is open. Before this task, pressing Escape while History/Settings/About was open silently wiped the user's in-progress calculation underneath the still-open panel (a pre-existing but previously-unnoticed bug, since Escape did nothing to the panel itself). Simply adding Escape-to-close on top of that would have made it worse (close the panel *and* wipe the calculation, both from one keypress). Fixed by adding a guard at the top of `useCalculator.ts`'s keydown handler: if any `[role="dialog"][aria-modal="true"]` element exists in the document, the calculator's own keyboard shortcuts (including Escape/`allClear`) are skipped entirely, so a panel being open now correctly hands the keyboard over to the panel (Escape closes *only* the panel; the calculator's expression underneath is left untouched) instead of both firing at once.
  - Confirmed `InstallBanner.tsx`'s existing `role="dialog"` (from Task 6) intentionally has no `aria-modal` — it's a non-blocking bottom banner, not an overlay, so it correctly does *not* trip the new calculator-keyboard guard (which only checks `aria-modal="true"`), and confirmed via `grep` that no CSS rule anywhere selects on `[role="dialog"]`/`[aria-modal]`, so the new attributes have no unintended styling side effects.
- **Systematic sweep of the remaining review checklist items**, each read/verified rather than assumed clean:
  - Console/runtime hygiene: `grep`'d all of `src/` for stray `console.log/warn/error` outside `__tests__` — none found.
  - Hydration-safety: audited every `typeof window`/`new Date()`/`Math.random()` usage across `page.tsx`, all calculator components, and every hook — all `typeof window` guards are inside effects/event handlers (not render), and the one `new Date().getFullYear()` render-time call (`AboutPanel.tsx`'s copyright line) is server/client-identical for any given day, so it carries no hydration-mismatch risk.
  - PWA/manifest: validated `public/manifest.json` parses as valid JSON and its 10-entry icon set matches files actually present in `public/`; confirmed `public/sw.js`'s precache list (`icon-192/512`, both maskable icons, `apple-touch-icon.png`) all exist on disk; re-confirmed every icon/splash asset referenced from `layout.tsx` (favicon, 16/32/48/72/96/128/144/152/180/192/384/512 PNGs, both maskable variants, `mask-icon.svg`, all nine `apple-touch-startup-image` splash PNGs) is present in `public/`.
  - Branding consistency: re-ran `grep -rniE "ahmed|auric"` across `src/`/`public/`/`README.md` — the only matches remaining are the correct "Ahmed Group of Companies" full legal name in `AboutPanel.tsx`/`SettingsPanel.tsx`, and the internal, non-user-facing `localStorage` keys (`ahmed-calc:*`) deliberately preserved since Task 7A to avoid wiping existing users' saved settings/history on update — both correct as-is.
  - Export formats: re-confirmed (via `grep`) that `exportHistoryCsv`/`Txt`/`Json`/`Xlsx`/`Docx`/`Pdf` in `src/lib/exportHistory.ts` are untouched and that `package.json` no longer lists the now-unused `xlsx` package (removed in Task 7D) — nothing in this task's changes touches any export path.
  - CSS/responsiveness: reviewed `globals.css`'s existing overflow/viewport-cap rules (`max-width: calc(100vw - Npx)` guards on the CurrencySelect and export dropdowns from Task 6) — all still in place and unaffected by this task's changes, which are confined to React logic and two ARIA attributes, not layout.
- Re-ran the standalone `tsc` syntax/type pass specifically against every file this task touched (`use-mobile.ts`, `useEscapeToClose.ts`, `useCalculator.ts`, `carousel.tsx`, `SettingsPanel.tsx`, `AboutPanel.tsx`, `HistoryPanel.tsx`) after all edits — zero real errors (only the same pre-existing environment-only noise present across every file in the project, confirmed identical before/after). Ran a brace/paren-balance check on each changed file (all balanced; `useCalculator.ts`'s naive counter shows an apparent paren mismatch that traces to parenthetical text inside comments elsewhere in the file, not a real syntax issue — `tsc` itself reports the file clean).
- Diffed the entire project tree against the Task 7E upload (`diff -rq`, excluding `node_modules`/`.next`): confirmed exactly 7 files changed (`tsconfig.json`; `src/hooks/use-mobile.ts`, `useCalculator.ts`; `src/components/ui/carousel.tsx`; `src/components/calculator/SettingsPanel.tsx`, `AboutPanel.tsx`, `HistoryPanel.tsx`) and one new file added (`src/hooks/useEscapeToClose.ts`) — nothing else in the project, including every export-format file, every icon/splash asset, and all Task 1–7E calculator/converter/history/settings/about logic, was touched.
